SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "Projects" AS p ON t."ProjectId" = p."Id"
LEFT JOIN "SimCardPlans" AS s0 ON t."SimCardPlanId" = s0."Id"
LEFT JOIN "SimProviders" AS s1 ON t."SimProviderId" = s1."Id"
LEFT JOIN "SimTypes" AS s2 ON t."SimTypeId" = s2."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t1.c, t1."FirstName", t1."LastName", t1.c0, t1."SimCardId"
    FROM (
        SELECT TRUE AS c, e0."FirstName", e0."LastName", 1 AS c0, e."SimCardId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY e."SimCardId" ORDER BY e."Id", e0."Id") AS row
        FROM "EmployeeSimCards" AS e
        INNER JOIN "Employees" AS e0 ON e."EmployeeId" = e0."Id"
        WHERE e."Status" = 1
    ) AS t1
    WHERE t1.row <= 1
) AS t0 ON t."Id" = t0."SimCardId"
ORDER BY t."SimAccountNo"

FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid

SELECT CASE WHEN COUNT(*) = 0 THEN FALSE ELSE TRUE END
FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
                    WHERE relname='pg_class' AND ns.nspname='pg_catalog'
                ) AND
                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')
        )

        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND

FROM pg_class AS cls
JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace
WHERE
        cls.relkind IN ('r', 'v', 'm', 'f', 'p') AND
        ns.nspname NOT IN ('pg_catalog', 'information_schema') AND
        -- Exclude tables which are members of PG extensions
        NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM pg_depend WHERE
                classid=(
                    SELECT cls.oid
                    FROM pg_class AS cls
                             JOIN pg_namespace AS ns ON ns.oid = cls.relnamespace

                objid=cls.oid AND
                deptype IN ('e', 'x')

2025-10-17 18:42:08.997 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (13ms) [Parameters=[@__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."Code", t."Name", t."Description", t."Status", CASE
    WHEN c."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN c."Name"
    ELSE ''
END AS "CompanyName", c0."Name" AS "CostCenterName", n."Name" AS "NationalityName", (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM "Employees" AS e
    WHERE e."ProjectId" = t."Id") AS "EmployeeCount"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Code", p."CompanyId", p."CostCenterId", p."Description", p."Name", p."NationalityId", p."Status"
    FROM "Projects" AS p
    ORDER BY p."Name"
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "Companies" AS c ON t."CompanyId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN "CostCenters" AS c0 ON t."CostCenterId" = c0."Id"
LEFT JOIN "Nationalities" AS n ON t."NationalityId" = n."Id"
ORDER BY t."Name"

    WHEN c."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN c."Name"
    ELSE ''
END AS "CompanyName", c0."Name" AS "CostCenterName", n."Name" AS "NationalityName", (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM "Employees" AS e
    WHERE e."ProjectId" = t."Id") AS "EmployeeCount"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Code", p."CompanyId", p."CostCenterId", p."Description", p."Name", p."NationalityId", p."Status"

    ORDER BY p."Name"
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t

SELECT t."Id", t."Code", t."Name", t."Description", t."Status", CASE
    WHEN c."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN c."Name"
    ELSE ''
END AS "CompanyName", c0."Name" AS "CostCenterName", n."Name" AS "NationalityName", (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM "Employees" AS e
    WHERE e."ProjectId" = t."Id") AS "EmployeeCount"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Code", p."CompanyId", p."CostCenterId", p."Description", p."Name", p."NationalityId", p."Status"
    FROM "Projects" AS p
    ORDER BY p."Name"
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "Companies" AS c ON t."CompanyId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN "CostCenters" AS c0 ON t."CostCenterId" = c0."Id"
LEFT JOIN "Nationalities" AS n ON t."NationalityId" = n."Id"
ORDER BY t."Name"

2025-10-17 18:53:52.738 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (24ms) [Parameters=[@__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."Code", t."Name", t."Description", t."Status", CASE
    WHEN c."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN c."Name"
    ELSE ''
END AS "CompanyName", c0."Name" AS "CostCenterName", n."Name" AS "NationalityName", (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM "Employees" AS e
    WHERE e."ProjectId" = t."Id") AS "EmployeeCount"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Code", p."CompanyId", p."CostCenterId", p."Description", p."Name", p."NationalityId", p."Status"
    FROM "Projects" AS p
    ORDER BY p."Name"
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "Companies" AS c ON t."CompanyId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN "CostCenters" AS c0 ON t."CostCenterId" = c0."Id"
LEFT JOIN "Nationalities" AS n ON t."NationalityId" = n."Id"
ORDER BY t."Name"

SELECT t."Id", t."Code", t."Name", t."Description", t."Status", CASE
    WHEN c."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN c."Name"
    ELSE ''
END AS "CompanyName", c0."Name" AS "CostCenterName", n."Name" AS "NationalityName", (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM "Employees" AS e
    WHERE e."ProjectId" = t."Id") AS "EmployeeCount"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Code", p."CompanyId", p."CostCenterId", p."Description", p."Name", p."NationalityId", p."Status"
    FROM "Projects" AS p
    ORDER BY p."Name"
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "Companies" AS c ON t."CompanyId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN "CostCenters" AS c0 ON t."CostCenterId" = c0."Id"
LEFT JOIN "Nationalities" AS n ON t."NationalityId" = n."Id"
ORDER BY t."Name"

SELECT t."Id", t."Code", t."Name", t."Description", t."Status", CASE
    WHEN c."Id" IS NOT NULL THEN c."Name"
    ELSE ''
END AS "CompanyName", c0."Name" AS "CostCenterName", n."Name" AS "NationalityName", (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM "Employees" AS e
    WHERE e."ProjectId" = t."Id") AS "EmployeeCount"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Code", p."CompanyId", p."CostCenterId", p."Description", p."Name", p."NationalityId", p."Status"
    FROM "Projects" AS p
    ORDER BY p."Name"
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN "Companies" AS c ON t."CompanyId" = c."Id"
LEFT JOIN "CostCenters" AS c0 ON t."CostCenterId" = c0."Id"

ORDER BY t."Name"

    ORDER BY a."AssetTag"

) AS t

LEFT JOIN "Projects" AS p ON t."ProjectId" = p."Id"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t1.c, t1."FirstName", t1."LastName", t1.c0, t1."AssetId"

        SELECT TRUE AS c, e0."FirstName", e0."LastName", 1 AS c0, e."AssetId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY e."AssetId" ORDER BY e."Id", e0."Id") AS row
